# End Event
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.928
	title = diggy_dungeons.928.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.928.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

    immediate = {
        dungeon_immediate_effect = yes
    }

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = floor_explored }
	}

    # All to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Infantry unit and manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.b
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.c
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to the field
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.e
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Fuck them
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.f
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		owner = { 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = dwarovar_expedition_douche
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = dont_pay_the_difference_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}

}

	id = diggy_dungeons.947
	title = diggy_dungeons.947.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.947.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.947.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

		dungeon_encounter_effect = {
			base_success = 80
			success_id = 949 # Spiders running your way: Fight (E) - Success
			
			base_failure = 20
			failure_id = 948 # Spiders running your way: Fight (E) - Failure
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.947.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {owner = {culture_group = goblin}}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 80
				success_id = 951 # Spiders running your way: Study Them (M) - Success
				
				base_failure = 20
				failure_id = 950 # Spiders running your way: Study Them (M) - Failure
			}
		}
		else = {
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 60
				success_id = 951 # Spiders running your way: Study Them (M) - Success
				
				base_failure = 40
				failure_id = 950 # Spiders running your way: Study Them (M) - Failure
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = diggy_dungeons.960
	title = diggy_dungeons.960.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.960.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.960.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = yidablaerun_2_counter
					value = 3
				}
			}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 100
				success_id = 963 # Running: Try to leave (H) - Success
				
				base_failure = 0
				failure_id = 964 # Hiding: Try to leave (H) - Failure
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = yidablaerun_2_counter
					value = 2
				}
			}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 80
				success_id = 963 # Running: Try to leave (H) - Success
				
				base_failure = 20
				failure_id = 964 # Hiding: Try to leave (H) - Failure
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = yidablaerun_2_counter
					value = 1
				}
			}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 60
				success_id = 963 # Running: Try to leave (H) - Success
				
				base_failure = 40
				failure_id = 964 # Hiding: Try to leave (H) - Failure
			}
		}
		else = {
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 40
				success_id = 963 # Running: Try to leave (H) - Success
				
				base_failure = 60
				failure_id = 964 # Hiding: Try to leave (H) - Failure
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.960.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { partySupplies = 4 }
		}
		change_party_supplies = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 4 }
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = yidablaerun_2_counter
				value = 1
			}
		}
		dungeon_progress_advancement = { id = 960 } # Hiding
	}
}

# End Event
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.966
	title = diggy_dungeons.966.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.966.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

    immediate = {
        dungeon_immediate_effect = yes
    }

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = floor_explored }
	}

    # All to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Infantry unit and manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.b
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.c
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to the field
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.e
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Fuck them
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.f
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		owner = { 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = dwarovar_expedition_douche
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = dont_pay_the_difference_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}

}

	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.968.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { partySupplies = 4 }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = yidablaerun_3_empower }
		}
		change_party_supplies = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 4 }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = yidablaerun_3_counter
					value = 1
				}
			}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 60
				success_id = 970 # Preparations: Empower Ourselves (E) - Success
				
				base_failure = 40
				failure_id = 972 # Preparations: Empower Ourselves (E) - Failure
			}
		}
		else = {
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 80
				success_id = 970 # Preparations: Empower Ourselves (E) - Success
				
				base_failure = 20
				failure_id = 972 # Preparations: Empower Ourselves (E) - Failure
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.968.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { partySupplies = 4 }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = yidablaerun_3_trap }
		}
		change_party_supplies = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 4 }

		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = {
					which = yidablaerun_3_counter
					value = 1
				}
			}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 60
				success_id = 971 # Preparations: Set up Traps (E) - Success
				
				base_failure = 40
				failure_id = 972 # Preparations: Empower Ourselves (E) - Failure
			}
		}
		else = {
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 80
				success_id = 971 # Preparations: Set up Traps (E) - Success
				
				base_failure = 20
				failure_id = 972 # Preparations: Empower Ourselves (E) - Failure
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.968.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

		dungeon_progress_advancement = { id = 969 } # Yidab Fight #1
	}
}

# End Event
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.998
	title = diggy_dungeons.998.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.998.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

    immediate = {
        dungeon_immediate_effect = yes
    }

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = floor_explored }
	}

    # All to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Infantry unit and manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.b
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.c
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to the field
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.e
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Fuck them
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.f
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		owner = { 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = dwarovar_expedition_douche
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = dont_pay_the_difference_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}

}

# Yidab's Nest
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.1000
	title = diggy_dungeons.1000.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1000.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1000.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {has_province_flag = yidablaerun_4_loot}
		}
		hidden_effect = {set_province_flag = yidablaerun_4_loot}
		dungeon_encounter_effect = {
			base_success = 60
			success_id = 1003 # Yidab's Nest: Loot her Cave (M) - Success
			
			base_failure = 40
			failure_id = 1004 # Yidab's Nest: Loot her Cave (M) - Failure
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1000.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = {has_province_flag = yidablaerun_4_loot}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 40
				success_id = 1001 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Success
				
				base_failure = 60
				failure_id = 1002 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Failure
			}
		}
		else = {
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 60
				success_id = 1001 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Success
				
				base_failure = 40
				failure_id = 1002 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Failure
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1000.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { partySupplies = 4 }
		}
		change_party_supplies = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 4 }
		if = {
			limit = {has_province_flag = yidablaerun_4_loot}
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 60
				success_id = 1001 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Success
				
				base_failure = 40
				failure_id = 1002 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Failure
			}
		}
		else = {
			dungeon_encounter_effect = {
				base_success = 80
				success_id = 1001 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Success
				
				base_failure = 20
				failure_id = 1002 # Yidab's Nest: Rush Forwards (M) - Failure
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.1010
	title = diggy_dungeons.1010.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1010.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	id = diggy_dungeons.1011
	title = diggy_dungeons.1011.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1011.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1011.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

			base_success = 60

		}

# End Event
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.1020
	title = diggy_dungeons.1020.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1020.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

    immediate = {
        dungeon_immediate_effect = yes
    }

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { set_province_flag = floor_explored }
		clr_province_flag = explorable_dungeon
		set_global_flag = dd_yidablaerun_4_completed
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = I98_bestiary_yidab
		}
	}

    # All to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.a
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Infantry unit and manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.b
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = treasury cash = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = adm_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = dip_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		currency_effect_expedition = {  currency = mil_power mana = yes addTo = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		custom_tooltip = base_expedition_loot_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to manpower
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.c
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Pay them, back to the field
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.e
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			while = {
				limit = { check_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 } }
				subtract_variable = { partyManpower = 1000 }
				owner = { infantry = PREV }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 1 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = pay_the_difference_tooltip
		currency_effect_expedition = { currency = treasury badLoot = yes takeFrom = owner }
		custom_tooltip = back_to_manpower_unit_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}
	
	# Fuck them
	option = {
        name = diggy_expedition.12.f
        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = { hidden_trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { partyLoot = 1 } } } }
		special_reward_expedition = yes
		owner = { 
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = dwarovar_expedition_douche
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = dont_pay_the_difference_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ancientDwarvenKnowledge = 1 } }
			province_event = { id = diggy_expedition.14 }
		}
		else = { hidden_effect = { clear_expedition_effect = yes } }
	}

}

# Yidab Fight #3
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.1021
	title = diggy_dungeons.1021.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1021.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1021.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

		dungeon_encounter_effect = {
			base_success = 40
			success_id = 1023 # Yidab Fight #3: Prepare Defenses (H) - Success
			
			base_failure = 60
			failure_id = 1022 # Yidab Fight #3: Prepare Defenses (H) - Failure
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1021.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

		dungeon_encounter_effect = {
			base_success = 60
			success_id = 1025 # Yidab Fight #3: All out Attack (M) - Success
			
			base_failure = 40
			failure_id = 1024 # Yidab Fight #3: All out Attack (M) - Failure
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1021.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}

		dungeon_progress_advancement = { id = 1010 } # Attempt to tame Yidab
	}
}

# Yidab Fight #3: Prepare Defenses (H) - Failure
province_event = {
	id = diggy_dungeons.1022
	title = diggy_dungeons.1022.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1022.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1022.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		change_party_manpower = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 200 }
		change_party_morale = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 1.5 }

		dungeon_progress_advancement = { id = 1005 } # Yidab Fight #1
	}
}

# Yidab Fight #3: Prepare Defenses (H) - Success

	id = diggy_dungeons.1023
	title = diggy_dungeons.1023.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.1023.d
	picture = TRADEGOODS_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = sent_expedition_@owner
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = expedition_death_timer }
	}

	option = {
		name = diggy_dungeons.1023.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		change_party_morale = { add_tooltip = yes add = 0.5 }
		change_party_supplies = { remove_tooltip = yes loss = 4 }
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = yidablaerun_4_battle_counter
				value = 1
			}
		}
		dungeon_progress_advancement = { id = 1005 } # Yidab Fight #1
	}
}

	id = diggy_dungeons.1026
	title = diggy_dungeons.2000.t
	desc = diggy_dungeons.2000.d
	picture = CAVE_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

        name = diggy_dungeons.2000.a

		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = dd_yidablaerun } }
			dungeon_ownership_reset_effect = yes
		}
	}
}
